<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $(".blogEntry-51039-error").hide();

        $(".attach-blogEntry-51039-to-contest-link").click(function () {
            Codeforces.facebox(".attach-blogEntry-51039-to-contest-form-holder", "http://st.codeforces.com/s/91331");

            $("#facebox .attach-blogEntry-51039-to-contest-form").submit(function () {
                if ($(this).find(":disabled").length === 0) {
                    $("#facebox .blogEntry-51039-error").hide();
                    $("#facebox #blogEntry-51039-resource-submitting-indicator").show();
                    $("#facebox #blogEntry-51039-resource-submit").attr("disabled", "disabled");

                    //noinspection JSUnusedGlobalSymbols
                    $.post("/data/blogAndContest?action=attachBlogToContest", {
                        blogId:"39427", contestId:$("#facebox #blogEntry-51039-contestId").val(),
                        blogEntryId:"51039",
                        resourceType:$("#facebox #blogEntry-51039-resourceType").val()
                    }, function (json) {
                        var validated = true;

                        for (var key in json) {
                            if (json.hasOwnProperty(key) && key.indexOf("error__") === 0) {
                                validated = false;
                                $("#facebox .blogEntry-51039-" + key.substring("error__".length) + "-error").show();
                                $("#facebox .for__blogEntry-51039-" + key.substring("error__".length)).text(json[key]);
                            }
                        }

                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-51039-resource-submitting-indicator").hide();
                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-51039-resource-submit").removeAttr("disabled");

                        if (validated) {
                            $.facebox.close();
                            if (json["success"] === "true") {
                                Codeforces.showMessage("Blog has been successfully attached to selected contest");
                            } else {
                                Codeforces.showMessage("There is unexpected error while attaching blog to the contest");
                            }
                        }
                    }, "json");
                }

                return false;
            });

            var contestSelect = $("#blogEntry-51039-contestId");
            var popupContestSelect = $("#facebox #blogEntry-51039-contestId");

            if (popupContestSelect.is(":disabled")) {
                $.post("/data/contests?action=getContestListWithEditableResources", function (data) {
                    if (data["result"] === "success") {
                        var contests = data["contests"];

                        for (var i = 0, contestCount = contests.length; i < contestCount; ++i) {
                            //noinspection StringLiteralBreaksHTMLJS
                            var contestOptionHtml = "<option value=\"" + contests[i]["id"] + "\">"
                                    + contests[i]["id"] + " - " + contests[i]["name"] + "</option>";
                            contestSelect.append(contestOptionHtml);
                            popupContestSelect.append(contestOptionHtml);
                        }

                        contestSelect.removeAttr("disabled");
                        $("#blogEntry-51039-contestId-loading-indicator").hide();
                        $("#blogEntry-51039-resource-submit").removeAttr("disabled");

                        popupContestSelect.removeAttr("disabled");
                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-51039-contestId-loading-indicator").hide();
                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-51039-resource-submit").removeAttr("disabled");
                    } else {
                        alert("Can't receive contest list");
                    }
                }, "json");
            }

            return false;
        });
    });
</script>

    <div class="content">
        <div class="ttypography"><p>Hello.</p><p>The round 1 of VK Cup 2017 will take place on March 18 at 18:35 MSK (check your timezone <a href="https://www.timeanddate.com/worldclock/fixedtime.html?day=18&amp;month=3&amp;year=2017&amp;hour=18&amp;min=35&amp;sec=0&amp;p1=166">here</a>), along with standard div1+2 Codeforces Round #405. The contest &quot;VK Cup 2017  Round 1&quot; is for teams qualified from two Qualification Rounds. The top 400 teams will advance to the Round 2, while other ones will have one more chance in the Wild Card Round 1 in April. Those who don't participate in the VK Cup can take part in the Codeforces Round #405 individually (problems will be available in English too). All three rounds last 2 hours, and all are rated.</p><p>I want to thank: <a class="rated-user user-red" href="/profile/KAN" title="Grandmaster KAN">KAN</a> for his help in the contest preparation, <a class="rated-user user-admin" href="/profile/MikeMirzayanov" title="Headquarters, MikeMirzayanov">MikeMirzayanov</a> that we are here, <a class="rated-user user-violet" href="/profile/AlexFetisov" title="Candidate Master AlexFetisov">AlexFetisov</a> for testing, the VK company for this nice annual contest.</p><p>I'm a setter and I hope (and expect?) that you will enjoy the problems. During the contest, remember that you can read many problems and try to solve those that fit you most.</p><p>I wish you great fun and no frustrating bugs.</p><p>div2: 500-1000-1500-2000-2500<br />div1: 500-1000-1500- <strong>2250</strong> -2500<br />vk-cup: <strong>250</strong>-500-1000-1500- <strong>2250</strong> -2500</p><p>The contest is over. See the editorial <a href="http://codeforces.com/blog/entry/51068">here</a>.                 $.post("/data/contests?action=getContestListWithEditableResources", function (data) {

                        for (var i = 0, contestCount = contests.length; i < contestCount; ++i) {

                        alert("Can't receive contest list");

                }, "json");

            return false;

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $(".blogEntry-50798-error").hide();

        $(".attach-blogEntry-50798-to-contest-link").click(function () {
            Codeforces.facebox(".attach-blogEntry-50798-to-contest-form-holder", "http://st.codeforces.com/s/91331");

            $("#facebox .attach-blogEntry-50798-to-contest-form").submit(function () {
                if ($(this).find(":disabled").length === 0) {
                    $("#facebox .blogEntry-50798-error").hide();
                    $("#facebox #blogEntry-50798-resource-submitting-indicator").show();
                    $("#facebox #blogEntry-50798-resource-submit").attr("disabled", "disabled");

                    //noinspection JSUnusedGlobalSymbols
                    $.post("/data/blogAndContest?action=attachBlogToContest", {
                        blogId:"1", contestId:$("#facebox #blogEntry-50798-contestId").val(),
                        blogEntryId:"50798",
                        resourceType:$("#facebox #blogEntry-50798-resourceType").val()
                    }, function (json) {
                        var validated = true;

                        for (var key in json) {
                            if (json.hasOwnProperty(key) && key.indexOf("error__") === 0) {
                                validated = false;
                                $("#facebox .blogEntry-50798-" + key.substring("error__".length) + "-error").show();
                                $("#facebox .for__blogEntry-50798-" + key.substring("error__".length)).text(json[key]);
                            }
                        }

                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-50798-resource-submitting-indicator").hide();
                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-50798-resource-submit").removeAttr("disabled");

                        if (validated) {
                            $.facebox.close();
                            if (json["success"] === "true") {
                                Codeforces.showMessage("Blog has been successfully attached to selected contest");
                            } else {
                                Codeforces.showMessage("There is unexpected error while attaching blog to the contest");
                            }
                        }
                    }, "json");
                }

                return false;
            });

            var contestSelect = $("#blogEntry-50798-contestId");
            var popupContestSelect = $("#facebox #blogEntry-50798-contestId");

            if (popupContestSelect.is(":disabled")) {
                $.post("/data/contests?action=getContestListWithEditableResources", function (data) {
                    if (data["result"] === "success") {
                        var contests = data["contests"];

                        for (var i = 0, contestCount = contests.length; i < contestCount; ++i) {
                            //noinspection StringLiteralBreaksHTMLJS
                            var contestOptionHtml = "<option value=\"" + contests[i]["id"] + "\">"
                                    + contests[i]["id"] + " - " + contests[i]["name"] + "</option>";
                            contestSelect.append(contestOptionHtml);
                            popupContestSelect.append(contestOptionHtml);
                        }

                        contestSelect.removeAttr("disabled");
                        $("#blogEntry-50798-contestId-loading-indicator").hide();
                        $("#blogEntry-50798-resource-submit").removeAttr("disabled");

                        popupContestSelect.removeAttr("disabled");
                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-50798-contestId-loading-indicator").hide();
                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-50798-resource-submit").removeAttr("disabled");
                    } else {
                        alert("Can't receive contest list");
                    }
                }, "json");
            }

            return false;
        });
    });
</script>

                        if (validated) {
                            $.facebox.close();
                            if (json["success"] === "true") {
                                Codeforces.showMessage("Blog has been successfully attached to selected contest");
                            } else {
                                Codeforces.showMessage("There is unexpected error while attaching blog to the contest");
                            }
                        }
                    }, "json");
                }

                return false;
            });

            var contestSelect = $("#blogEntry-50708-contestId");
            var popupContestSelect = $("#facebox #blogEntry-50708-contestId");

            if (popupContestSelect.is(":disabled")) {
                $.post("/data/contests?action=getContestListWithEditableResources", function (data) {
                    if (data["result"] === "success") {
                        var contests = data["contests"];

                        for (var i = 0, contestCount = contests.length; i < contestCount; ++i) {
                            //noinspection StringLiteralBreaksHTMLJS
                            var contestOptionHtml = "<option value=\"" + contests[i]["id"] + "\">"
                                    + contests[i]["id"] + " - " + contests[i]["name"] + "</option>";
                            contestSelect.append(contestOptionHtml);
                            popupContestSelect.append(contestOptionHtml);
                        }

                        contestSelect.removeAttr("disabled");
                        $("#blogEntry-50708-contestId-loading-indicator").hide();
                        $("#blogEntry-50708-resource-submit").removeAttr("disabled");

                        popupContestSelect.removeAttr("disabled");
                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-50708-contestId-loading-indicator").hide();
                        $("#facebox #blogEntry-50708-resource-submit").removeAttr("disabled");
                    } else {
                        alert("Can't receive contest list");
                    }
                }, "json");
            }

            return false;
        });
    });
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
                // Create new ':containsIgnoreCase' selector for search
                jQuery.expr[':'].containsIgnoreCase = function(a, i, m) {
                    return jQuery(a).text().toUpperCase()
                            .indexOf(m[3].toUpperCase()) >= 0;
                };

                if (window.updateDatatableFilter == undefined) {
                    window.updateDatatableFilter = function(i) {
                        var parent = $(i).parent().parent().parent().parent();
                        $("tr.no-items", parent).remove();
                        $("tr", parent).hide().removeClass('visible');
                        var text = $(i).val();
                        if (text) {
                            $("tr" + ":containsIgnoreCase('" + text + "')", parent).show().addClass('visible');
                        } else {
                            parent.find(".rowCount").text("");
                            $("tr", parent).show().addClass('visible');
                        }

                        var found = false;
                        var visibleRowCount = 0;
                        $("tr", parent).each(function () {
                            if (!found) {
                                if ($(this).find("th").size() > 0) {
                                    $(this).show().addClass('visible');
                                    found = true;
                                }
                            }
                            if ($(this).hasClass('visible')) {
                                visibleRowCount++;
                            }
                        });
                        if (text) {
                            parent.find(".rowCount").text("Matches: " + (visibleRowCount - (found ? 1 : 0)));
                        }
                        if (visibleRowCount == (found ? 1 : 0)) {
                            $("<tr class='no-items visible'><td style=\"text-align:left;\"colspan=\"32\">No items<\/td><\/tr>").appendTo($(parent).find('table'));
                        }
                        $(parent).find("tr td").removeClass("dark");
                        $(parent).find("tr.visible:odd td").addClass("dark");
                    }

                    $(".datatable .closed").click(function () {
                        var parent = $(this).parent();
                        $(this).hide();
                        $(".filter", parent).fadeIn(function () {
                            $("input", parent).val("").focus().css("border", "1px solid #aaa");
                        });
                    });

                    $(".datatable .opened").click(function () {
                        var parent = $(this).parent().parent();
                        $(".filter", parent).fadeOut(function () {
                            $(".closed", parent).show();
                            $("input", parent).val("").each(function () {
                                window.updateDatatableFilter(this);
                            });
                        });
                    });

                    $(".datatable .filter input").keyup(function(e) {
                        window.updateDatatableFilter(this);
                        e.preventDefault();
                        e.stopPropagation();
                    });

                    $(".datatable table").each(function () {
                        var found = false;
                        $("tr", this).each(function () {
                            if (!found && $(this).find("th").size() == 0) {
                                found = true;
                            }
                        });
                        if (!found) {
                            $("<tr class='no-items visible'><td style=\"text-align:left;\"colspan=\"32\">No items<\/td><\/tr>").appendTo(this);
                        }
                    });

                    // Applies styles to datatables.
                    $(".datatable").each(function () {
                        $(this).find("tr:first th").addClass("top");
                        $(this).find("tr:last td").addClass("bottom");
                        $(this).find("tr:odd td").addClass("dark");
                        $(this).find("tr td:first-child, tr th:first-child").addClass("left");
                        $(this).find("tr td:last-child, tr th:last-child").addClass("right");
                    });

                    $(".datatable table.tablesorter").each(function () {
                        $(this).bind("sortEnd", function () {
                            $(".datatable").each(function () {
                                $(this).find("th, td")
                                    .removeClass("top").removeClass("bottom")
                                    .removeClass("left").removeClass("right")
                                    .removeClass("dark");
                                $(this).find("tr:first th").addClass("top");
                                $(this).find("tr:last td").addClass("bottom");
                                $(this).find("tr:odd td").addClass("dark");
                                $(this).find("tr td:first-child, tr th:first-child").addClass("left");
                                $(this).find("tr td:last-child, tr th:last-child").addClass("right");
                            });
                        });
                    });
                }
        });
    </script>
            </div>

        <script type="application/javascript">
            $(function() {
                $(".userListMarker").click(function() {
                    $.post("/data/lists", {action: "findTouched"}, function(json) {
                        Codeforces.facebox(".userListsFacebox");
                        var tbody = $("#facebox tbody");
                        tbody.empty();
                        for (var i in json) {
                            tbody.append(
                                    $("<tr></tr>").append(
                                            $("<td></td>").attr("data-readKey", json[i].readKey).text(json[i].name)
                                    )
                            );
                        }
                        Codeforces.updateDatatables();
                        tbody.find("td").css("cursor", "pointer").click(function() {
                            document.location = Codeforces.updateUrlParameter(document.location.href, "list", $(this).attr("data-readKey"));
                        });
                    }, "json");
                });
            });

<!-- share popup -->
<script type="text/javascript">
(function($) {
  $(document).on( 'click', '.share-bar .icon', function(e) {
    /*************Open Shares in New Window Code**********/
    e.preventDefault();
    console.log('share url');
    var url = $(this).attr('href');
    cb_popupCenter(url,'shareWindow','600', '600');
  });

  function cb_popupCenter(url, title, w, h) {
    // http://stackoverflow.com/questions/4068373/center-a-popup-window-on-screen
    var dualScreenLeft = window.screenLeft != undefined ? window.screenLeft : screen.left;
    var dualScreenTop = window.screenTop != undefined ? window.screenTop : screen.top;

    var width = window.innerWidth ? window.innerWidth : document.documentElement.clientWidth ? document.documentElement.clientWidth : screen.width;
    var height = window.innerHeight ? window.innerHeight : document.documentElement.clientHeight ? document.documentElement.clientHeight : screen.height;

    var left = ((width / 2) - (w / 2)) + dualScreenLeft;
    var top = ((height / 2) - (h / 2)) + dualScreenTop;
    var newWindow = window.open(url, title, 'scrollbars=yes, width=' + w + ', height=' + h + ', top=' + top + ', left=' + left);

    // Puts focus on the newWindow
    if (window.focus) {
        newWindow.focus();
    }
  }
})(jQuery);
</script>
<!-- end share popup -->

				  window.onload = (typeof window.onload != 'function') ?
					 loadChartbeat : function() { try { oldonload(); } catch (e) { loadChartbeat(); throw e} loadChartbeat(); };
				})();
